            def markdown(text)
        
      156. 
      
        
    156. 
          
          
              options = {
        
      157. 
      
        
    157. 
          
          
                autolink: true,
        
      158. 
      
        
    158. 
          
          
                filter_html: true,
        
      159. 
      
        
    159. 
          
          
                hard_wrap: true,
        
      160. 
      
        
    160. 
          
          
                link_attributes: { rel: 'nofollow', target: '_blank' },
        
      161. 
      
        
    161. 
          
          
                space_after_headers: true,
        
      162. 
      
        
    162. 
          
          
                fenced_code_blocks: true
        
      163. 
      
        
    163. 
          
          
              }
        
      164. 
      
        
    164. 
          
          
              extensions = {
        
      165. 
      
        
    165. 
          
          
                autolink: true,
        
      166. 
      
        
    166. 
          
          
                superscript: true,
        
      167. 
      
        
    167. 
          
          
                disable_indented_code_blocks: true
        
      168. 
      
        
    168. 
          
          
              }
        
      169. 
      
        
    169. 
          
          
              renderer = Redcarpet::Render::HTML.new(options)
        
      170. 
      
        
    170. 
          
          
              markdown = Redcarpet::Markdown.new(renderer, extensions)
        
      171. 
      
        
    171. 
          
          
              markdown.render(text).html_safe
        
      172. 
      
        
    172. 
          
          
            end

            def errors_for(resource)
        
      179. 
      
        
    179. 
          
          
              rc = ''
        
      180. 
      
        
    180. 
          
          
              if resource.errors.any?
        
      181. 
      
        
    181. 
          
          
          
        
      182. 
      
        
    182. 
          
          
                rc += "<div id='error_explanation'>" \
        
      183. 
      
        
    183. 
          
          
                      '<ul>' +
        
      184. 
      
        
    184. 
          
          
                      resource.errors.full_messages.map do |msg|
        
      185. 
      
        
    185. 
          
          
                        '<li><b>' + msg.split(' ', 2)[0] + '</b>: ' + msg.split(' ', 2)[1] + '</li>'
        
      186. 
      
        
    186. 
          
          
                      end.join
        
      187. 
      
        
    187. 
          
          
                if defined? resource.attachments
        
      188. 
      
        
    188. 
          
          
                  rc.each do |attr|
        
      189. 
      
        
    189. 
          
          
                    errors.delete(attr) unless attrs_to_retain.include?(attr)
        
      190. 
      
        
    190. 
          
          
                  end
        
      191. 
      
        
    191. 
          
          
                  rc += '<ul>' +
        
      192. 
      
        
    192. 
          
          
                        resource.attachments.map do |p|
        
      193. 
      
        
    193. 
          
          
                          p.errors.map do |error|
        
      194. 
      
        
    194. 
          
          
                            '<li>' + p.errors[error].join(', '.html_safe) + '</li>'
        
      195. 
      
        
    195. 
          
          
                          end.join
        
      196. 
      
        
    196. 
          
          
                        end.join +
        
      197. 
      
        
    197. 
          
          
                        '</ul>'
        
      198. 
      
        
    198. 
          
          
                end
        
      199. 
      
        
    199. 
          
          
                rc += '</ul></div>'
        
      200. 
      
        
    200. 
          
          
          
        
      201. 
      
        
    201. 
          
          
                rc.html_safe
        
      202. 
      
        
    202. 
          
          
              end
        
      203. 
      
        
    203. 
          
          
            end

            def present(model, presenter_class = nil)

              klass = presenter_class || "#{model.class}Presenter".constantize
        
      238.

      239.

            def self.conver_size_to_array(size)
        
      106.

              return [] unless size

    117.

      118.
